I've reproduced the issue. The problem occurs when runes mode is enabled. Now let me understand the issue better by looking at the ClassBody.js file again:\n\nLooking at the ClassBody.js file, the issue is clear:\n1. On line 16, it checks if `context.state.analysis.runes` is enabled, and only processes class members if runes mode is active.\n2. Great! I've reproduced the issue. The problem occurs when runes mode is enabled. Now let me understand the issue better by looking at the ClassBody.js file again:

Looking at the ClassBody.js file, the issue is clear:
1. On line 16, it checks if `context.state.analysis.runes` is enabled, and only processes class members if runes mode is active.
2. On line 79, for PropertyDefinition, it checks `!child.static` to only process non-static properties.
3. However, on lines 90-123, for MethodDefinition, there's no check for `child.static`, so both static and non-static methods are being added to the same `fields` Map with the same key.

The fix is to include the static flag in the key used to track fields, or to skip static methods similar to how static properties are skipped. Looking at the code, I think the best approach is to include the static flag in the key, so that static and non-static members with the same name don't conflict.

// Final comprehensive verification script for the static class member fix
import { compile } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/compiler/index.js'"'"';

let passed = 0;
let failed = 0;

function testCase(name, code, shouldFail = false) {
  try {
    const result = compile(code, { 
      filename: '"'"'test.svelte'"'"',
      generate: '"'"'client'"'"'
    });
    if (shouldFail) {
      console.log(`❌ ${name} - Expected error but succeeded`);
      failed++;
    } else {
      console.log(`✓ ${name}`);
      passed++;
    }
  } catch (error) {
    if (shouldFail) {
      console.log(`✓ ${name}`);
      passed++;
    } else {
      console.log(`❌ ${name} - Unexpected error: ${error.code}`);
      failed++;
    }
  }
}

console.log('"'"'=== Testing Static Class Member Fix ===\n'"'"');

// Main test from PR description
testCase(
  '"'"'PR Issue: Static and instance methods with same name'"'"',
  `<script>
let count = $state(0);
class Hello {
  hello() {}
  static hello() {}
}
</script>`,
  false
);

// Test various combinations
testCase(
  '"'"'Static and instance properties'"'"',
  `<script>
let count = $state(0);
class Hello {
  foo = 1;
  static foo = 2;
}
</script>`,
  false
);

testCase(
  '"'"'Static property and instance method'"'"',
  `<script>
let count = $state(0);
class Hello {
  static foo = 1;
  foo() {}
}
</script>`,
  false
);

testCase(
  '"'"'Instance property and static method'"'"',
  `<script>
let count = $state(0);
class Hello {
  foo = 1;
  static foo() {}
}
</script>`,
  false
);

testCase(
  '"'"'Static and instance getters/setters'"'"',
  `<script>
let count = $state(0);
class Hello {
  get value() { return 1; }
  set value(v) {}
  static get value() { return 2; }
  static set value(v) {}
}
</script>`,
  false
);

// Tests that should still fail
testCase(
  '"'"'Duplicate instance methods (should fail)'"'"',
  `<script>
let count = $state(0);
class Hello {
  hello() {}
  hello() {}
}
</script>`,
  true
);

testCase(
  '"'"'Duplicate static methods (should fail)'"'"',
  `<script>
let count = $state(0);
class Hello {
  static hello() {}
  static hello() {}
}
</script>`,
  true
);

testCase(
  '"'"'Duplicate instance properties (should fail)'"'"',
  `<script>
let count = $state(0);
class Hello {
  foo = 1;
  foo = 2;
}
</script>`,
  true
);

testCase(
  '"'"'Duplicate static properties (should fail)'"'"',
  `<script>
let count = $state(0);
class Hello {
  static foo = 1;
  static foo = 2;
}
</script>`,
  true
);

testCase(
  '"'"'Instance method and property conflict (should fail)'"'"',
  `<script>
let count = $state(0);
class Hello {
  foo() {}
  foo = 1;
}
</script>`,
  true
);

testCase(
  '"'"'Static method and property conflict (should fail)'"'"',
  `<script>
let count = $state(0);
class Hello {
  static foo() {}
  static foo = 1;
}
</script>`,
  true
);

// Test with state runes
testCase(
  '"'"'State rune in instance property with static method'"'"',
  `<script>

  foo = $state(1);
  static foo() {}
}
</script>`,
  false
);

// Complex case

  '"'"'Complex class with multiple static and instance members'"'"',
  `<script>

class Hello {
  name = '"'"'instance'"'"';

  get value() { return 1; }

}

  false

+
+        /** @type {Map<string, StateField>} */
+        const state_fields = new Map();
+
+        /** @type {Map<string, Array<MethodDefinition['kind'] | 'prop' | 'assigned_prop'>>} */
+        const fields = new Map();
+
+        context.state.analysis.classes.set(node, state_fields);
+
+        /** @type {MethodDefinition | null} */
+        let constructor = null;
+
+        /**
+         * @param {PropertyDefinition | AssignmentExpression} node
+         * @param {Expression | PrivateIdentifier} key
+         * @param {Expression | null | undefined} value
+         */
+        function handle(node, key, value) {
+                const name = get_name(key);
+                if (name === null) return;
+
+                const rune = get_rune(value, context.state.scope);
+
+                if (rune && is_state_creation_rune(rune)) {
+                        if (state_fields.has(name)) {
+                                e.state_field_duplicate(node, name);
+                        }
+
+                        const _key = (key.type === 'PrivateIdentifier' ? '#' : '') + name;
+                        const field = fields.get(_key);
+
+                        // if there's already a method or assigned field, error
+                        if (field && !(field.length === 1 && field[0] === 'prop')) {
+                                e.duplicate_class_field(node, _key);
+                        }
+
+                        state_fields.set(name, {
+                                node,
+                                type: rune,
+                                // @ts-expect-error for public state this is filled out in a moment
+                                key: key.type === 'PrivateIdentifier' ? key : null,
+                                value: /** @type {CallExpression} */ (value)
+                        });
+                }
+        }
+
+        for (const child of node.body) {
+                if (child.type === 'PropertyDefinition' && !child.computed) {
+                        // Only handle state runes for non-static properties
+                        if (!child.static) {
+                                handle(child, child.key, child.value);
+                        }
+                        // Include static flag in the key to allow same names for static and non-static members
+                        const name = get_name(child.key);
+                        const key = (child.static ? 'static:' : '') + (child.key.type === 'PrivateIdentifier' ? '#' : '') + name;
+                        const field = fields.get(key);
+                        if (!field) {
+                                fields.set(key, [child.value ? 'assigned_prop' : 'prop']);
+                                continue;
+                        }
+                        // Use a cleaner name for the error message
+                        const error_name = (child.key.type === 'PrivateIdentifier' ? '#' : '') + name;
+                        e.duplicate_class_field(child, error_name);
+                }
+
+                if (child.type === 'MethodDefinition') {
+                        if (child.kind === 'constructor') {
+                                constructor = child;
+                        } else if (!child.computed) {
+                                // Include static flag in the key to allow same names for static and non-static members
+                                const name = get_name(child.key);
+                                const key = (child.static ? 'static:' : '') + (child.key.type === 'PrivateIdentifier' ? '#' : '') + name;
+                                const field = fields.get(key);
+                                if (!field) {
+                                        fields.set(key, [child.kind]);
+                                        continue;
+                                }
+                                if (
+                                        field.includes(child.kind) ||
+                                        field.includes('prop') ||
+                                        field.includes('assigned_prop')
+                                ) {
+                                        // Use a cleaner name for the error message
+                                        const error_name = (child.key.type === 'PrivateIdentifier' ? '#' : '') + name;
+                                        e.duplicate_class_field(child, error_name);
+                                }
+                                if (child.kind === 'get') {
+                                        if (field.length === 1 && field[0] === 'set') {
+                                                field.push('get');
+                                                continue;
+                                        }
+                                } else if (child.kind === 'set') {
+                                        if (field.length === 1 && field[0] === 'get') {
+                                                field.push('set');
+                                                continue;
+                                        }
+                                } else {
+                                        field.push(child.kind);
+                                        continue;
+                                }
+                                // Use a cleaner name for the error message
+                                const error_name = (child.key.type === 'PrivateIdentifier' ? '#' : '') + name;
+                                e.duplicate_class_field(child, error_name);
+                        }
+                }
+        }
+
+        if (constructor) {
+                for (const statement of constructor.value.body.body) {
+                        if (statement.type !== 'ExpressionStatement') continue;
+                        if (statement.expression.type !== 'AssignmentExpression') continue;
+
+                        const { left, right } = statement.expression;
+
+                        if (left.type !== 'MemberExpression') continue;
+                        if (left.object.type !== 'ThisExpression') continue;
+                        if (left.computed && left.property.type !== 'Literal') continue;
+
+                        handle(statement.expression, left.property, right);
+                }
+        }
+
+        for (const [name, field] of state_fields) {
+                if (name[0] === '#') {
+                        continue;
+                }
+
+                let deconflicted = name.replace(regex_invalid_identifier_chars, '_');
+                while (private_ids.includes(deconflicted)) {
+                        deconflicted = '_' + deconflicted;
+                }
+
+                private_ids.push(deconflicted);
+                field.key = b.private_id(deconflicted);
+        }
+
+        context.next({ ...context.state, state_fields });
 }

+                const rune = get_rune(value, context.state.scope);
+
+                if (rune && is_state_creation_rune(rune)) {
+                        if (state_fields.has(name)) {
+                                e.state_field_duplicate(node, name);
+                        }
+
+                        const _key = (key.type === 'PrivateIdentifier' ? '#' : '') + name;
+                        const field = fields.get(_key);
+
+                        // if there's already a method or assigned field, error
+                        if (field && !(field.length === 1 && field[0] === 'prop')) {
+                                e.duplicate_class_field(node, _key);
+                        }
+
+                        state_fields.set(name, {
+                                node,
+                                type: rune,
+                                // @ts-expect-error for public state this is filled out in a moment
+                                key: key.type === 'PrivateIdentifier' ? key : null,
+                                value: /** @type {CallExpression} */ (value)
+                        });
+                }
+        }
+
+        for (const child of node.body) {
+                if (child.type === 'PropertyDefinition' && !child.computed) {
+                        // Only handle state runes for non-static properties
+                        if (!child.static) {
+                                handle(child, child.key, child.value);
+                        }
+                        // Include static flag in the key to allow same names for static and non-static members
+                        const name = get_name(child.key);
+                        const key = (child.static ? 'static:' : '') + (child.key.type === 'PrivateIdentifier' ? '#' : '') + name;
+                        const field = fields.get(key);
+                        if (!field) {
+                                fields.set(key, [child.value ? 'assigned_prop' : 'prop']);
+                                continue;
+                        }
+                        // Use a cleaner name for the error message
+                        const error_name = (child.key.type === 'PrivateIdentifier' ? '#' : '') + name;
+                        e.duplicate_class_field(child, error_name);
+                }
+
+                if (child.type === 'MethodDefinition') {
+                        if (child.kind === 'constructor') {
+                                constructor = child;
+                        } else if (!child.computed) {
+                                // Include static flag in the key to allow same names for static and non-static members
+                                const name = get_name(child.key);
+                                const key = (child.static ? 'static:' : '') + (child.key.type === 'PrivateIdentifier' ? '#' : '') + name;
+                                const field = fields.get(key);
+                                if (!field) {
+                                        fields.set(key, [child.kind]);
+                                        continue;
+                                }
+                                if (
+                                        field.includes(child.kind) ||
+                                        field.includes('prop') ||
+                                        field.includes('assigned_prop')
+                                ) {
+                                        // Use a cleaner name for the error message
+                                        const error_name = (child.key.type === 'PrivateIdentifier' ? '#' : '') + name;
+                                        e.duplicate_class_field(child, error_name);
+                                }
+                                if (child.kind === 'get') {
+                                        if (field.length === 1 && field[0] === 'set') {
+                                                field.push('get');
+                                                continue;
+                                        }
+                                } else if (child.kind === 'set') {
+                                        if (field.length === 1 && field[0] === 'get') {
+                                                field.push('set');
+                                                continue;
+                                        }
+                                } else {
+                                        field.push(child.kind);
+                                        continue;
+                                }
+                                // Use a cleaner name for the error message
+                                const error_name = (child.key.type === 'PrivateIdentifier' ? '#' : '') + name;
+                                e.duplicate_class_field(child, error_name);
+                        }
+                }
+        }
+
+        if (constructor) {
+                for (const statement of constructor.value.body.body) {
+                        if (statement.type !== 'ExpressionStatement') continue;
+                        if (statement.expression.type !== 'AssignmentExpression') continue;
+
+                        const { left, right } = statement.expression;
+
+                        if (left.type !== 'MemberExpression') continue;
+                        if (left.object.type !== 'ThisExpression') continue;
+                        if (left.computed && left.property.type !== 'Literal') continue;
+
+                        handle(statement.expression, left.property, right);
+                }
+        }
+
+        for (const [name, field] of state_fields) {
+                if (name[0] === '#') {
+                        continue;
+                }
+
+                let deconflicted = name.replace(regex_invalid_identifier_chars, '_');
+                while (private_ids.includes(deconflicted)) {
+                        deconflicted = '_' + deconflicted;
+                }
+
+                private_ids.push(deconflicted);
+                field.key = b.private_id(deconflicted);
+        }
+
+        context.next({ ...context.state, state_fields });
 }
